 On its doodle, Google showed Mukesh with a smiling face, depicting a scene from the late director Yash Chopra's most popular romantic film Kabhi Kabhi Kabhi

 Motilal, a distant relative of Mukesh and a well-known Bollywood actor, recognized the singer skills

 After this Motilal trained Mukesh in music with Pandit Jagannath Prasad

 el

 Akshaya Tritiya has special significance in Hinduism
 ise akha teej bhi kaha jaataa he
 Every year Tritiya of Shukla Paksha of Vaishakh month is called Akshaya Tritiya
 is baar akshay tritiya 18 april ko he or is din aap kai shubh kaary kar sakate hai
 This time there will be Akshaya Tritiya from sunrise to 3:03 pm
 vaise to kaha jaataa he ki har maheene kii shukla paksh kii tritiy shubh hoti he, lekin akshay tritiya kaa khaas mahatv he
 The literal meaning of Akshay is never decayed, that is to remain permanent
 sthai vahiin rah saktaa jo sarvada satya he
 It can be said with certainty that truth is only the divine which is renewable, unbroken and comprehensive
 yah akshay tritiya tithi ishwar tithi he
 This Akshaya Tithi is also called Parshuram Tithi because it is Parshuram's birthday
 is din hota he grahon ko shubh sanyog- is din grahon kaa vishesh sanyog banataa he
 - Sun and Moon are in their highest zodiac sign
 - saal main sirf ek din ye sanyog banataa he
 - Sun is in Aries and Moon is in Taurus
 - shastron main surya ko hamaara praan or chandramaa ko hamaara man mana gaya he
 - Due to the relationship between Sun and Moon, this date becomes very important
 - isliye is din jo bhi kaam kiya jaae uskaa fal doguna or kabhi na khatm hone vaala hoga
 In the event of being inauspicious, give these signs on this day
 Do these auspicious tasks on this day: - Akshaya Tritiya can be done related to wedding, home-entry, purchase of clothes and jewelry or purchase of house, land, car
 - is din nayaa kapadaa, jevar pahananaa or nai sanstha or kaam kaa udghaatan shubh mana jaataa he
 - It is a mythological belief that on this day, the tarpan and pinddan or any kind of donation made to the ancestral side gives akshaya
 - is din kiya gaya ganga snaan or pujan sabhi paapon ko nasht karata he
 Eat plenty of cantaloupe in the month of Vaishakh, and also donate - Every person wishes for prosperity
 isi vajah se is din sona kharidne se vah akshay matlab kabhi na khatm hone vaala hoga
 - The chanting, penance, havan, puja, donation performed on Akshaya Tritiya increases manifold
 - is din hamen sadgunon ke liye prarthana kerani chahie or jane anjaane main kiye gaye paapon kii kshamaa yachana kerani chahie

 - input IANS Today is the death anniversary of Savitribai Phule
 unka nidhan 10 march 1897 ke din hua tha
 He is known to work for women
 unka janm ek dalit parivaar main 3 janvari, 1831 main maharashtra ke satara main ek chota se gaanvnayganvamen hua tha
 At the age of just 9, she was married to Jyotirao Phule, 13 years old
 jaanate hai unke bare main kuch khaas baaten
 Savitribai Phule, despite social discrimination and many obstacles, completed her education and pioneered to educate the rest of the women
 -savitribai phule ko bharat kii pehali mahila adhyapika or nari mukti andolan kii pehali netaa kaha jaataa he
 Veer of Rajouri: Had broken bones, yet kept fighting - She, along with her husband revolutionary leader Jyotirao Phule, had opened 18 schools for girls
 pehla skool 1848 main pune balika vidhyalay kholaa tha
 Savitribai opposed such malpractices prevalent in the society, especially against women
 unhone satipratha, bal-vivaah or vidhwaa vivaah nishedh ke khilaaf aawaaj uthaai or jeevanaparyant usee ke liye ladati raheen

 uskaa naam yashavanth raav rakhaa
 Made him a doctor after reading and writing

 On 28 January 1853, he set up a Child Murder Restrictive Home for pregnant rape victims
 - savitribai ne unnisvin sadi main chuaa-chhot, satipratha, bal-vivaah or vidhwaa vivaah nishedh jaisi kureetiyaan ke viruddh apane pati ke saath milakar kaam kiya

 ) India and Japan signed a bilateral currency swap agreement of 75 billion dollars on Monday
 isse desh kii videshi karency or puunji bazaar main sthirataa aane kii ummid he
 The $ 75 billion deal is the world's largest swap (exchange) agreement
 pradhanmantrinarendra modiki japan yatra ke dauraan yah samjhauta kiya gaya, jahaan unhone japani pradhanmantri shinjo abe ke saath kii muddon par baat kii
 The government said that it is taking several steps to stop the capital from going out of the country and this decision is a step to increase confidence in the Indian market
 gauratlab he ki america main pramukh byaaj daron main badhotaree se puunji par behatar laabh ke liye duniya bhar ke niveshak bhartiya bazaar main lagaai apni puunji teji se nikaal rahe hai or america bazaaron main nivesh badha rahe hai
 This has also affected the strength of the Indian rupee
 rupaya main or giravat na ho, iske liye japan ke saath swap samjhaute ko hari jhandi di gai he
 What is the Currency Swap Arrangement (CSA) The currency swap agreement between India and Japan on Monday is called Currency Swap Arrangement (CSA)
 isse pehle 20 se zyada deshon ke saath bharat kaa aisa samjhauta he
 The CSA takes place between two friendly countries that have strong bilateral relations
 aise do deshon ke bich kaarobaari sambandh bhi majboot hote hai
 So this agreement is done for both the countries to do business in their local currency
 antarrashtriya str par kaarobaar yaa to dollar main hote hai yauromen
 The strength and fall of both these currencies have an impact on the business of other countries
 isse bachane ke liye siese jaise samjhaute kiye jate hai
 Under the CSA, the two countries negotiated pay the amount of imports or exports only at the rate of the fixed currency
 iske liye kisi tisare desh ke karency, masalan dollar yaa euro kii madad nahin leni padati he
 Simply put, the importer or exporter has to bid for the goods in their local currency
 teesraa paksh is kaarobaar main shaamil nahin hota, isliye videsh mudra ke vinimay (exange) ke jhanjhat se chhutkaaraa mil jaataa he
 Which countries with India's CSA are mostly oil selling countries
 agrani tel niryaatak deshon main angola, algeria, nigeria, iran, iraq, oman, katar, venezuela, saudi arab or yaman jaise desh hai jiske saath bharat kaa siese he
 There are also some countries with which oil exports are not concerned, but India has a CSA with them
 in deshon main japan, rus, australia, dakshin korea jaise desh hai
 Also Singapore
 indonesia, malaysia, mexico, dakshin africa or thailand bhi hai jinke saath siese he
 Decreased dependence on the dollar The biggest advantage of CSA will be that the third country currency will not be used in business
 jab do desh apni sthaneey karency main deal karenge to dollar yaa euro kii jarurat nahin padegi
 Due to this, the movement of these two major currencies will not affect the business of other countries
 philhal kai videshi niveshak bharat se apana paisa nikaalkar america main daal rahe hai jisase dollar majboot hua he or rupaya gira he
 Now when two countries do business in local currency, there will be no need for dollars and import or export will also not prove to be very expensive
 bharat ke saath china kaa sambandhchin kai varshon se chahta he ki bharat ke saath yuan main vyapaar ho
 For this, CSA has to be done between the two countries but India is not ready for this at the moment
 china kii daleel he ki yuan main kaarobaar hone se bharat main chini paryatakon kii sankhya badhegi jo philhal kaaphi kam he
 India can also increase China's foreign exchange and it will also have the benefit of employment in the service sector, but India is not moving forward on this agreement due to security and trade deficit

 aapako bataa den ki hamaari ankhen solah chitron ko dekhakar isamen antar kar sakati he
